Minecraft structure resembling a traditional East Asian pagoda or temple with the following features:

A two-story wooden building with ornate, upward-curving roofs on each level.
The structure is primarily made of dark oak wood blocks and planks.
Each floor is approximately 5 blocks tall, with the ground floor slightly taller.
The building is about 15 blocks wide and 10 blocks deep.
The roof of each level is constructed with a combination of dark oak stairs and green terracotta or concrete blocks, creating a layered effect with upturned corners.
The walls feature a pattern of dark oak frames filled with white concrete or wool blocks, creating a distinctive contrast.
The ground floor has a central entrance flanked by dark oak pillars and fences creating a porch-like area.
The second floor has a balcony with dark oak fences as railings.
Lanterns hang from the corners of each roof level.
The building is elevated on a platform made of dark oak planks, accessible by stairs.
Surrounding the structure is a garden area with a mix of grass, coarse dirt, and terracotta paths.
Various plants, including flowers and custom-made trees, are placed around the building.
